            <p class="intro" style="white-space: pre-line">
                                                <br>
                    做起来很简单 夏天胃口不好，这样的海鲜粥再合适不过！食材可以根据自己的情况调整，山药要戴着手套操作不然手会很痒
给孩子吃不用加白胡椒，大人吃加一点会更好吃哦
                                                                <br>
                    
参与活动:
                                                                                        <a href="https://m.douguo.com/activity/ncpzj/detail/4035?isapp=1&amp;open=0&amp;_vs=1000300&amp;&amp;dg_refreshkey=publishnote" style="color:#35CEAC;" target="_blank">#食在清明|寻找春天的鲜味#</a>
                                    </p>

                <!-- 步骤 -->
                <div class="step">
            <h2 class="mini-title">干贝虾仁粥的做法</h2>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement2" data-snum="2" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/yuan_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/yuan_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/200_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解1" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤1</p>
                    干贝提前三小时冷藏泡发备用，山药要戴手套处理切成丁，胡萝卜切丁。其他材料洗净备用，青菜叶切碎
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement3" data-snum="3" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/yuan_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/yuan_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/200_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解2" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤2</p>
                    锅里加水800克，煮开加入80克大米中火边搅拌边煮，煮到粘稠状。加生抽跟糖调味
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement4" data-snum="4" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/yuan_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/yuan_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/200_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解3" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤3</p>
                    加入干贝，虾仁，山药，姜丝，青豆，胡萝卜，蟹腿菇，全部倒入锅里。中火煮三分钟。要一直搅拌。
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement5" data-snum="5" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/yuan_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/yuan_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/200_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解4" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤4</p>
                    最后放入青菜叶，搅拌均匀，加松鲜鲜香油。大人可以加白胡椒主要是去腥増鲜，小孩可以选择不加。
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement6" data-snum="6" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/yuan_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/yuan_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/200_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解5" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤5</p>
                    完成
                </div>
            </div>
                    </div>
                        <!-- 小贴士 -->

    function showShareBox(thiz,type){
        $(thiz).addClass('active');
        $('.share_info').removeClass('wechat weibo qq');
        if(type == 1){
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至微信');
            $('.share_info').addClass('wechat');
        } else if(type == 2){
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至微博');
            $('.share_info').addClass('weibo');
        }else{
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至QQ');
            $('.share_info').addClass('qq');
        }
        $('.share_info').show();
    }
    function hideShareBox(thiz,type){
        $(thiz).removeClass('active');
        $('.share_info').hide();
    }
    var comments = '';

        $.ajax({
            url: "/login/user",

                comments.getCommentList(0,3);
                // getCommentsNum();
            }
        })
        // $.ajax({
        //     url: "/cookformat/"+"3300888",

        //     success:function(res) {
        //         $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+res.data);

        function getCommentsNum(){
            var data = { type: 'cook', 'id': 3300888, sort: "desc" };
            $.ajax({
                url: '/comment/list/0/3',

    function getNowDate () {
        var compareDate = new Date("2024-04-10 14:05:36");
        var currentDate = new Date();
        var timeDiff = currentDate.getTime() - compareDate.getTime();
        var secondsDiff = Math.floor(timeDiff / 1000);
        return secondsDiff;
    }

    function nowDateEnd(){
        var now = new Date("2024-04-10 14:05:36");
        var hours = now.getHours();
        var minutes = now.getMinutes();
        var seconds = now.getSeconds();
        var totalSeconds = (hours * 60 * 60) + (minutes * 60) + seconds;
        var secondDiff = (24 * 60 * 60) - totalSeconds;
        return secondDiff;
    }
    let nowdate = getNowDate();
    let $timeDiff = nowdate; //发布时间距离当前时间的差值(秒数)
    let nowDateEnds = nowDateEnd();
    let $secondDiff = nowDateEnds; //发布时间距离第二天的差值

    if($timeDiff < 60){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+'刚刚');
    }

    if($timeDiff < 3600){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+round($timeDiff / 60)+'分钟前');
    }

    if($timeDiff < 86400){
        if($timeDiff > $secondDiff){
            $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ '1天前');
        }
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ round($timeDiff / 3600)+'小时前');
    }
    if($timeDiff < $secondDiff + 86400*7){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ Math.ceil(($timeDiff - $secondDiff) / 86400)+'天前');
    }
</script>

                <div class="step">
            <h2 class="mini-title">干贝虾仁粥的做法</h2>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement2" data-snum="2" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/yuan_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/yuan_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/200_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解1" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤1</p>
                    干贝提前三小时冷藏泡发备用，山药要戴手套处理切成丁，胡萝卜切丁。其他材料洗净备用，青菜叶切碎
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement3" data-snum="3" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/yuan_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/yuan_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/200_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解2" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤2</p>
                    锅里加水800克，煮开加入80克大米中火边搅拌边煮，煮到粘稠状。加生抽跟糖调味
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement4" data-snum="4" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/yuan_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/yuan_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/200_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解3" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤3</p>
                    加入干贝，虾仁，山药，姜丝，青豆，胡萝卜，蟹腿菇，全部倒入锅里。中火煮三分钟。要一直搅拌。
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement5" data-snum="5" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/yuan_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/yuan_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/200_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解4" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤4</p>
                    最后放入青菜叶，搅拌均匀，加松鲜鲜香油。大人可以加白胡椒主要是去腥増鲜，小孩可以选择不加。
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement6" data-snum="6" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/yuan_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/yuan_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/200_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解5" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤5</p>
                    完成
                </div>
            </div>
                    </div>
                        <!-- 小贴士 -->
        <div class="tips">
            <h2 class="mini-title">干贝虾仁粥的烹饪技巧</h2>
            <p><br>做菜好吃都有技巧，我的每道菜都有小妙招，大家搜索“豆果”可以直接查看我的菜谱！</p>

    function showShareBox(thiz,type){
        $(thiz).addClass('active');
        $('.share_info').removeClass('wechat weibo qq');
        if(type == 1){
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至微信');
            $('.share_info').addClass('wechat');
        } else if(type == 2){
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至微博');
            $('.share_info').addClass('weibo');
        }else{
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至QQ');
            $('.share_info').addClass('qq');
        }
        $('.share_info').show();
    }
    function hideShareBox(thiz,type){
        $(thiz).removeClass('active');
        $('.share_info').hide();
    }

        function getCommentsNum(){

            $.ajax({

    function getNowDate () {
        var compareDate = new Date("2024-04-10 14:05:36");
        var currentDate = new Date();
        var timeDiff = currentDate.getTime() - compareDate.getTime();
        var secondsDiff = Math.floor(timeDiff / 1000);
        return secondsDiff;
    }

    function nowDateEnd(){
        var now = new Date("2024-04-10 14:05:36");
        var hours = now.getHours();
        var minutes = now.getMinutes();
        var seconds = now.getSeconds();
        var totalSeconds = (hours * 60 * 60) + (minutes * 60) + seconds;
        var secondDiff = (24 * 60 * 60) - totalSeconds;
        return secondDiff;
    }
    let nowdate = getNowDate();
    let $timeDiff = nowdate; //发布时间距离当前时间的差值(秒数)
    let nowDateEnds = nowDateEnd();
    let $secondDiff = nowDateEnds; //发布时间距离第二天的差值

    if($timeDiff < 60){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+'刚刚');
    }

    if($timeDiff < 3600){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+round($timeDiff / 60)+'分钟前');
    }

    if($timeDiff < 86400){
        if($timeDiff > $secondDiff){
            $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ '1天前');
        }
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ round($timeDiff / 3600)+'小时前');
    }
    if($timeDiff < $secondDiff + 86400*7){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ Math.ceil(($timeDiff - $secondDiff) / 86400)+'天前');
    }
</script>

            <p class="intro" style="white-space: pre-line">
                                                <br>
                    做起来很简单 夏天胃口不好，这样的海鲜粥再合适不过！食材可以根据自己的情况调整，山药要戴着手套操作不然手会很痒
给孩子吃不用加白胡椒，大人吃加一点会更好吃哦
                                                                <br>
                    
参与活动:

                <!-- 步骤 -->
                <div class="step">
            <h2 class="mini-title">干贝虾仁粥的做法</h2>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement2" data-snum="2" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/yuan_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/yuan_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/200_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解1" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤1</p>
                    干贝提前三小时冷藏泡发备用，山药要戴手套处理切成丁，胡萝卜切丁。其他材料洗净备用，青菜叶切碎
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement3" data-snum="3" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/yuan_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/yuan_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/200_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解2" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤2</p>
                    锅里加水800克，煮开加入80克大米中火边搅拌边煮，煮到粘稠状。加生抽跟糖调味
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement4" data-snum="4" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/yuan_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/yuan_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/200_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解3" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤3</p>
                    加入干贝，虾仁，山药，姜丝，青豆，胡萝卜，蟹腿菇，全部倒入锅里。中火煮三分钟。要一直搅拌。
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement5" data-snum="5" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/yuan_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/yuan_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/200_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解4" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤4</p>
                    最后放入青菜叶，搅拌均匀，加松鲜鲜香油。大人可以加白胡椒主要是去腥増鲜，小孩可以选择不加。
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement6" data-snum="6" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/yuan_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/yuan_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/200_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解5" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤5</p>
                    完成
                </div>
            </div>
                    </div>
                        <!-- 小贴士 -->

    function showShareBox(thiz,type){
        $(thiz).addClass('active');
        $('.share_info').removeClass('wechat weibo qq');
        if(type == 1){
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至微信');
            $('.share_info').addClass('wechat');
        } else if(type == 2){
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至微博');
            $('.share_info').addClass('weibo');
        }else{
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至QQ');
            $('.share_info').addClass('qq');
        }
        $('.share_info').show();
    }
    function hideShareBox(thiz,type){
        $(thiz).removeClass('active');
        $('.share_info').hide();
    }
    var comments = '';
    $(function(){
        $.ajax({
            url: "/login/user",
            data:"",
            success:function(res) {

                comments = new Comments("3300888",'cook',user,'wHsgB8jFmv7U8mQkkpyE4Zxi6yKHNNoeHcByDQnw',3,$('.readMore'));
                comments.getCommentList(0,3);
                // getCommentsNum();
            }
        })
        // $.ajax({
        //     url: "/cookformat/"+"3300888",
        //     data:"",
        //     success:function(res) {
        //         $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+res.data);
        //     }

        function getCommentsNum(){
            var data = { type: 'cook', 'id': 3300888, sort: "desc" };
            $.ajax({
                url: '/comment/list/0/3',
                type: 'get',
                data: data,

    function getNowDate () {
        var compareDate = new Date("2024-04-10 14:05:36");
        var currentDate = new Date();
        var timeDiff = currentDate.getTime() - compareDate.getTime();
        var secondsDiff = Math.floor(timeDiff / 1000);
        return secondsDiff;
    }

    function nowDateEnd(){
        var now = new Date("2024-04-10 14:05:36");
        var hours = now.getHours();
        var minutes = now.getMinutes();
        var seconds = now.getSeconds();
        var totalSeconds = (hours * 60 * 60) + (minutes * 60) + seconds;
        var secondDiff = (24 * 60 * 60) - totalSeconds;
        return secondDiff;
    }
    let nowdate = getNowDate();
    let $timeDiff = nowdate; //发布时间距离当前时间的差值(秒数)
    let nowDateEnds = nowDateEnd();
    let $secondDiff = nowDateEnds; //发布时间距离第二天的差值

    if($timeDiff < 60){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+'刚刚');
    }

    if($timeDiff < 3600){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+round($timeDiff / 60)+'分钟前');
    }

    if($timeDiff < 86400){
        if($timeDiff > $secondDiff){
            $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ '1天前');
        }
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ round($timeDiff / 3600)+'小时前');
    }
    if($timeDiff < $secondDiff + 86400*7){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ Math.ceil(($timeDiff - $secondDiff) / 86400)+'天前');
    }
</script>

                <!-- 步骤 -->
                <div class="step">
            <h2 class="mini-title">干贝虾仁粥的做法</h2>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement2" data-snum="2" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/yuan_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/yuan_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/200_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解1" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤1</p>
                    干贝提前三小时冷藏泡发备用，山药要戴手套处理切成丁，胡萝卜切丁。其他材料洗净备用，青菜叶切碎
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement3" data-snum="3" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/yuan_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/yuan_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/200_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解2" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤2</p>
                    锅里加水800克，煮开加入80克大米中火边搅拌边煮，煮到粘稠状。加生抽跟糖调味
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement4" data-snum="4" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/yuan_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/yuan_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/200_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解3" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤3</p>
                    加入干贝，虾仁，山药，姜丝，青豆，胡萝卜，蟹腿菇，全部倒入锅里。中火煮三分钟。要一直搅拌。
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement5" data-snum="5" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/yuan_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/yuan_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/200_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解4" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤4</p>
                    最后放入青菜叶，搅拌均匀，加松鲜鲜香油。大人可以加白胡椒主要是去腥増鲜，小孩可以选择不加。
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement6" data-snum="6" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/yuan_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/yuan_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/200_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解5" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤5</p>
                    完成
                </div>
            </div>
                    </div>
                        <!-- 小贴士 -->

    function showShareBox(thiz,type){
        $(thiz).addClass('active');
        $('.share_info').removeClass('wechat weibo qq');
        if(type == 1){
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至微信');
            $('.share_info').addClass('wechat');
        } else if(type == 2){
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至微博');
            $('.share_info').addClass('weibo');
        }else{
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至QQ');
            $('.share_info').addClass('qq');
        }
        $('.share_info').show();
    }
    function hideShareBox(thiz,type){
        $(thiz).removeClass('active');
        $('.share_info').hide();
    }

                comments.getCommentList(0,3);

        function getCommentsNum(){

    function getNowDate () {
        var compareDate = new Date("2024-04-10 14:05:36");
        var currentDate = new Date();
        var timeDiff = currentDate.getTime() - compareDate.getTime();
        var secondsDiff = Math.floor(timeDiff / 1000);
        return secondsDiff;
    }

    function nowDateEnd(){
        var now = new Date("2024-04-10 14:05:36");
        var hours = now.getHours();
        var minutes = now.getMinutes();
        var seconds = now.getSeconds();
        var totalSeconds = (hours * 60 * 60) + (minutes * 60) + seconds;
        var secondDiff = (24 * 60 * 60) - totalSeconds;
        return secondDiff;
    }
    let nowdate = getNowDate();
    let $timeDiff = nowdate; //发布时间距离当前时间的差值(秒数)
    let nowDateEnds = nowDateEnd();
    let $secondDiff = nowDateEnds; //发布时间距离第二天的差值

    if($timeDiff < 60){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+'刚刚');
    }

    if($timeDiff < 3600){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+round($timeDiff / 60)+'分钟前');
    }

    if($timeDiff < 86400){
        if($timeDiff > $secondDiff){
            $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ '1天前');
        }
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ round($timeDiff / 3600)+'小时前');
    }
    if($timeDiff < $secondDiff + 86400*7){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ Math.ceil(($timeDiff - $secondDiff) / 86400)+'天前');
    }
</script>

            <p class="intro" style="white-space: pre-line">
                                                <br>
                    做起来很简单 夏天胃口不好，这样的海鲜粥再合适不过！食材可以根据自己的情况调整，山药要戴着手套操作不然手会很痒
给孩子吃不用加白胡椒，大人吃加一点会更好吃哦

                <!-- 步骤 -->
                <div class="step">
            <h2 class="mini-title">干贝虾仁粥的做法</h2>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement2" data-snum="2" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/yuan_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/yuan_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/200_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解1" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤1</p>
                    干贝提前三小时冷藏泡发备用，山药要戴手套处理切成丁，胡萝卜切丁。其他材料洗净备用，青菜叶切碎
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement3" data-snum="3" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/yuan_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/yuan_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/200_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解2" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤2</p>
                    锅里加水800克，煮开加入80克大米中火边搅拌边煮，煮到粘稠状。加生抽跟糖调味
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement4" data-snum="4" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/yuan_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/yuan_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/200_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解3" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤3</p>
                    加入干贝，虾仁，山药，姜丝，青豆，胡萝卜，蟹腿菇，全部倒入锅里。中火煮三分钟。要一直搅拌。
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement5" data-snum="5" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/yuan_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/yuan_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/200_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解4" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤4</p>
                    最后放入青菜叶，搅拌均匀，加松鲜鲜香油。大人可以加白胡椒主要是去腥増鲜，小孩可以选择不加。
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement6" data-snum="6" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/yuan_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/yuan_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/200_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解5" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤5</p>
                    完成
                </div>
            </div>
                    </div>
                        <!-- 小贴士 -->

            <h2 class="mini-title">干贝虾仁粥的烹饪技巧</h2>
            <p><br>做菜好吃都有技巧，我的每道菜都有小妙招，大家搜索“豆果”可以直接查看我的菜谱！</p>

    function showShareBox(thiz,type){
        $(thiz).addClass('active');
        $('.share_info').removeClass('wechat weibo qq');
        if(type == 1){
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至微信');
            $('.share_info').addClass('wechat');
        } else if(type == 2){
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至微博');
            $('.share_info').addClass('weibo');
        }else{
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至QQ');
            $('.share_info').addClass('qq');
        }
        $('.share_info').show();
    }
    function hideShareBox(thiz,type){
        $(thiz).removeClass('active');
        $('.share_info').hide();
    }
    var comments = '';
    $(function(){
        $.ajax({
            url: "/login/user",
            data:"",
            success:function(res) {
                var user=res.data.user;
                comments = new Comments("3300888",'cook',user,'wHsgB8jFmv7U8mQkkpyE4Zxi6yKHNNoeHcByDQnw',3,$('.readMore'));
                comments.getCommentList(0,3);
                // getCommentsNum();
            }
        })
        // $.ajax({
        //     url: "/cookformat/"+"3300888",
        //     data:"",
        //     success:function(res) {
        //         $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+res.data);
        //     }
        // })
        function getCommentsNum(){
            var data = { type: 'cook', 'id': 3300888, sort: "desc" };
            $.ajax({
                url: '/comment/list/0/3',
                type: 'get',
                data: data,
                success: function success(res) {
                    var total = res.data.total;
                    if(total > 1){
                        $('.readMore').show();
                    }
                }
            });
        }
        $('.readMore').click(function(){
            $('.toast').show();
        })
    })
    function getNowDate () {
        var compareDate = new Date("2024-04-10 14:05:36");
        var currentDate = new Date();
        var timeDiff = currentDate.getTime() - compareDate.getTime();
        var secondsDiff = Math.floor(timeDiff / 1000);
        return secondsDiff;
    }

    function nowDateEnd(){
        var now = new Date("2024-04-10 14:05:36");
        var hours = now.getHours();
        var minutes = now.getMinutes();
        var seconds = now.getSeconds();
        var totalSeconds = (hours * 60 * 60) + (minutes * 60) + seconds;
        var secondDiff = (24 * 60 * 60) - totalSeconds;
        return secondDiff;
    }
    let nowdate = getNowDate();
    let $timeDiff = nowdate; //发布时间距离当前时间的差值(秒数)
    let nowDateEnds = nowDateEnd();
    let $secondDiff = nowDateEnds; //发布时间距离第二天的差值

    if($timeDiff < 60){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+'刚刚');
    }

    if($timeDiff < 3600){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+round($timeDiff / 60)+'分钟前');
    }

    if($timeDiff < 86400){
        if($timeDiff > $secondDiff){
            $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ '1天前');
        }
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ round($timeDiff / 3600)+'小时前');
    }
    if($timeDiff < $secondDiff + 86400*7){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ Math.ceil(($timeDiff - $secondDiff) / 86400)+'天前');
    }
</script>

            <p class="intro" style="white-space: pre-line">
                                                <br>
                    做起来很简单 夏天胃口不好，这样的海鲜粥再合适不过！食材可以根据自己的情况调整，山药要戴着手套操作不然手会很痒
给孩子吃不用加白胡椒，大人吃加一点会更好吃哦
                                                                <br>
                    
参与活动:
                                                                                        <a href="https://m.douguo.com/activity/ncpzj/detail/4035?isapp=1&amp;open=0&amp;_vs=1000300&amp;&amp;dg_refreshkey=publishnote" style="color:#35CEAC;" target="_blank">#食在清明|寻找春天的鲜味#</a>
                                    </p>

                <!-- 步骤 -->
                <div class="step">
            <h2 class="mini-title">干贝虾仁粥的做法</h2>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement2" data-snum="2" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/yuan_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/yuan_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/200_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解1" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤1</p>
                    干贝提前三小时冷藏泡发备用，山药要戴手套处理切成丁，胡萝卜切丁。其他材料洗净备用，青菜叶切碎
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement3" data-snum="3" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/yuan_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/yuan_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/200_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解2" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤2</p>
                    锅里加水800克，煮开加入80克大米中火边搅拌边煮，煮到粘稠状。加生抽跟糖调味
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement4" data-snum="4" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/yuan_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/yuan_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/200_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解3" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤3</p>
                    加入干贝，虾仁，山药，姜丝，青豆，胡萝卜，蟹腿菇，全部倒入锅里。中火煮三分钟。要一直搅拌。
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement5" data-snum="5" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/yuan_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/yuan_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/200_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解4" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤4</p>
                    最后放入青菜叶，搅拌均匀，加松鲜鲜香油。大人可以加白胡椒主要是去腥増鲜，小孩可以选择不加。
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement6" data-snum="6" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/yuan_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/yuan_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/200_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解5" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤5</p>
                    完成
                </div>
            </div>
                    </div>
                        <!-- 小贴士 -->

    function showShareBox(thiz,type){
        $(thiz).addClass('active');
        $('.share_info').removeClass('wechat weibo qq');
        if(type == 1){
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至微信');
            $('.share_info').addClass('wechat');
        } else if(type == 2){
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至微博');
            $('.share_info').addClass('weibo');
        }else{
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至QQ');
            $('.share_info').addClass('qq');
        }
        $('.share_info').show();
    }
    function hideShareBox(thiz,type){
        $(thiz).removeClass('active');
        $('.share_info').hide();
    }
    var comments = '';

        $.ajax({
            url: "/login/user",

                comments.getCommentList(0,3);
                // getCommentsNum();
            }
        })
        // $.ajax({
        //     url: "/cookformat/"+"3300888",

        //     success:function(res) {
        //         $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+res.data);

        function getCommentsNum(){
            var data = { type: 'cook', 'id': 3300888, sort: "desc" };
            $.ajax({
                url: '/comment/list/0/3',

    function getNowDate () {
        var compareDate = new Date("2024-04-10 14:05:36");
        var currentDate = new Date();
        var timeDiff = currentDate.getTime() - compareDate.getTime();
        var secondsDiff = Math.floor(timeDiff / 1000);
        return secondsDiff;
    }

    function nowDateEnd(){
        var now = new Date("2024-04-10 14:05:36");
        var hours = now.getHours();
        var minutes = now.getMinutes();
        var seconds = now.getSeconds();
        var totalSeconds = (hours * 60 * 60) + (minutes * 60) + seconds;
        var secondDiff = (24 * 60 * 60) - totalSeconds;
        return secondDiff;
    }
    let nowdate = getNowDate();
    let $timeDiff = nowdate; //发布时间距离当前时间的差值(秒数)
    let nowDateEnds = nowDateEnd();
    let $secondDiff = nowDateEnds; //发布时间距离第二天的差值

    if($timeDiff < 60){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+'刚刚');
    }

    if($timeDiff < 3600){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+round($timeDiff / 60)+'分钟前');
    }

    if($timeDiff < 86400){
        if($timeDiff > $secondDiff){
            $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ '1天前');
        }
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ round($timeDiff / 3600)+'小时前');
    }
    if($timeDiff < $secondDiff + 86400*7){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ Math.ceil(($timeDiff - $secondDiff) / 86400)+'天前');
    }
</script>

                <div class="step">
            <h2 class="mini-title">干贝虾仁粥的做法</h2>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement2" data-snum="2" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/yuan_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/yuan_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/200_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解1" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤1</p>
                    干贝提前三小时冷藏泡发备用，山药要戴手套处理切成丁，胡萝卜切丁。其他材料洗净备用，青菜叶切碎
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement3" data-snum="3" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/yuan_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/yuan_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/200_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解2" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤2</p>
                    锅里加水800克，煮开加入80克大米中火边搅拌边煮，煮到粘稠状。加生抽跟糖调味
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement4" data-snum="4" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/yuan_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/yuan_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/200_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解3" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤3</p>
                    加入干贝，虾仁，山药，姜丝，青豆，胡萝卜，蟹腿菇，全部倒入锅里。中火煮三分钟。要一直搅拌。
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement5" data-snum="5" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/yuan_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/yuan_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/200_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解4" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤4</p>
                    最后放入青菜叶，搅拌均匀，加松鲜鲜香油。大人可以加白胡椒主要是去腥増鲜，小孩可以选择不加。
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement6" data-snum="6" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/yuan_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/yuan_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/200_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解5" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤5</p>
                    完成
                </div>
            </div>
                    </div>
                        <!-- 小贴士 -->
        <div class="tips">
            <h2 class="mini-title">干贝虾仁粥的烹饪技巧</h2>
            <p><br>做菜好吃都有技巧，我的每道菜都有小妙招，大家搜索“豆果”可以直接查看我的菜谱！</p>

    function showShareBox(thiz,type){
        $(thiz).addClass('active');
        $('.share_info').removeClass('wechat weibo qq');
        if(type == 1){
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至微信');
            $('.share_info').addClass('wechat');
        } else if(type == 2){
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至微博');
            $('.share_info').addClass('weibo');
        }else{
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至QQ');
            $('.share_info').addClass('qq');
        }
        $('.share_info').show();
    }
    function hideShareBox(thiz,type){
        $(thiz).removeClass('active');
        $('.share_info').hide();
    }

        function getCommentsNum(){

            $.ajax({

    function getNowDate () {
        var compareDate = new Date("2024-04-10 14:05:36");
        var currentDate = new Date();
        var timeDiff = currentDate.getTime() - compareDate.getTime();
        var secondsDiff = Math.floor(timeDiff / 1000);
        return secondsDiff;
    }

    function nowDateEnd(){
        var now = new Date("2024-04-10 14:05:36");
        var hours = now.getHours();
        var minutes = now.getMinutes();
        var seconds = now.getSeconds();
        var totalSeconds = (hours * 60 * 60) + (minutes * 60) + seconds;
        var secondDiff = (24 * 60 * 60) - totalSeconds;
        return secondDiff;
    }
    let nowdate = getNowDate();
    let $timeDiff = nowdate; //发布时间距离当前时间的差值(秒数)
    let nowDateEnds = nowDateEnd();
    let $secondDiff = nowDateEnds; //发布时间距离第二天的差值

    if($timeDiff < 60){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+'刚刚');
    }

    if($timeDiff < 3600){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+round($timeDiff / 60)+'分钟前');
    }

    if($timeDiff < 86400){
        if($timeDiff > $secondDiff){
            $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ '1天前');
        }
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ round($timeDiff / 3600)+'小时前');
    }
    if($timeDiff < $secondDiff + 86400*7){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ Math.ceil(($timeDiff - $secondDiff) / 86400)+'天前');
    }
</script>

            <p class="intro" style="white-space: pre-line">
                                                <br>
                    做起来很简单 夏天胃口不好，这样的海鲜粥再合适不过！食材可以根据自己的情况调整，山药要戴着手套操作不然手会很痒
给孩子吃不用加白胡椒，大人吃加一点会更好吃哦
                                                                <br>
                    
参与活动:

                <!-- 步骤 -->
                <div class="step">
            <h2 class="mini-title">干贝虾仁粥的做法</h2>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement2" data-snum="2" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/yuan_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/yuan_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/200_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解1" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤1</p>
                    干贝提前三小时冷藏泡发备用，山药要戴手套处理切成丁，胡萝卜切丁。其他材料洗净备用，青菜叶切碎
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement3" data-snum="3" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/yuan_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/yuan_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/200_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解2" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤2</p>
                    锅里加水800克，煮开加入80克大米中火边搅拌边煮，煮到粘稠状。加生抽跟糖调味
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement4" data-snum="4" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/yuan_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/yuan_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/200_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解3" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤3</p>
                    加入干贝，虾仁，山药，姜丝，青豆，胡萝卜，蟹腿菇，全部倒入锅里。中火煮三分钟。要一直搅拌。
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement5" data-snum="5" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/yuan_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/yuan_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/200_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解4" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤4</p>
                    最后放入青菜叶，搅拌均匀，加松鲜鲜香油。大人可以加白胡椒主要是去腥増鲜，小孩可以选择不加。
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement6" data-snum="6" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/yuan_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/yuan_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/200_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解5" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤5</p>
                    完成
                </div>
            </div>
                    </div>
                        <!-- 小贴士 -->

    function showShareBox(thiz,type){
        $(thiz).addClass('active');
        $('.share_info').removeClass('wechat weibo qq');
        if(type == 1){
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至微信');
            $('.share_info').addClass('wechat');
        } else if(type == 2){
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至微博');
            $('.share_info').addClass('weibo');
        }else{
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至QQ');
            $('.share_info').addClass('qq');
        }
        $('.share_info').show();
    }
    function hideShareBox(thiz,type){
        $(thiz).removeClass('active');
        $('.share_info').hide();
    }
    var comments = '';
    $(function(){
        $.ajax({
            url: "/login/user",
            data:"",
            success:function(res) {

                comments = new Comments("3300888",'cook',user,'wHsgB8jFmv7U8mQkkpyE4Zxi6yKHNNoeHcByDQnw',3,$('.readMore'));
                comments.getCommentList(0,3);
                // getCommentsNum();
            }
        })
        // $.ajax({
        //     url: "/cookformat/"+"3300888",
        //     data:"",
        //     success:function(res) {
        //         $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+res.data);
        //     }

        function getCommentsNum(){
            var data = { type: 'cook', 'id': 3300888, sort: "desc" };
            $.ajax({
                url: '/comment/list/0/3',
                type: 'get',
                data: data,

    function getNowDate () {
        var compareDate = new Date("2024-04-10 14:05:36");
        var currentDate = new Date();
        var timeDiff = currentDate.getTime() - compareDate.getTime();
        var secondsDiff = Math.floor(timeDiff / 1000);
        return secondsDiff;
    }

    function nowDateEnd(){
        var now = new Date("2024-04-10 14:05:36");
        var hours = now.getHours();
        var minutes = now.getMinutes();
        var seconds = now.getSeconds();
        var totalSeconds = (hours * 60 * 60) + (minutes * 60) + seconds;
        var secondDiff = (24 * 60 * 60) - totalSeconds;
        return secondDiff;
    }
    let nowdate = getNowDate();
    let $timeDiff = nowdate; //发布时间距离当前时间的差值(秒数)
    let nowDateEnds = nowDateEnd();
    let $secondDiff = nowDateEnds; //发布时间距离第二天的差值

    if($timeDiff < 60){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+'刚刚');
    }

    if($timeDiff < 3600){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+round($timeDiff / 60)+'分钟前');
    }

    if($timeDiff < 86400){
        if($timeDiff > $secondDiff){
            $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ '1天前');
        }
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ round($timeDiff / 3600)+'小时前');
    }
    if($timeDiff < $secondDiff + 86400*7){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ Math.ceil(($timeDiff - $secondDiff) / 86400)+'天前');
    }
</script>

                <!-- 步骤 -->
                <div class="step">
            <h2 class="mini-title">干贝虾仁粥的做法</h2>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement2" data-snum="2" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/yuan_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/yuan_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/200_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解1" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤1</p>
                    干贝提前三小时冷藏泡发备用，山药要戴手套处理切成丁，胡萝卜切丁。其他材料洗净备用，青菜叶切碎
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement3" data-snum="3" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/yuan_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/yuan_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/200_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解2" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤2</p>
                    锅里加水800克，煮开加入80克大米中火边搅拌边煮，煮到粘稠状。加生抽跟糖调味
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement4" data-snum="4" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/yuan_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/yuan_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/200_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解3" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤3</p>
                    加入干贝，虾仁，山药，姜丝，青豆，胡萝卜，蟹腿菇，全部倒入锅里。中火煮三分钟。要一直搅拌。
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement5" data-snum="5" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/yuan_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/yuan_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/200_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解4" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤4</p>
                    最后放入青菜叶，搅拌均匀，加松鲜鲜香油。大人可以加白胡椒主要是去腥増鲜，小孩可以选择不加。
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement6" data-snum="6" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/yuan_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/yuan_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/200_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解5" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤5</p>
                    完成
                </div>
            </div>
                    </div>
                        <!-- 小贴士 -->

    function showShareBox(thiz,type){
        $(thiz).addClass('active');
        $('.share_info').removeClass('wechat weibo qq');
        if(type == 1){
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至微信');
            $('.share_info').addClass('wechat');
        } else if(type == 2){
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至微博');
            $('.share_info').addClass('weibo');
        }else{
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至QQ');
            $('.share_info').addClass('qq');
        }
        $('.share_info').show();
    }
    function hideShareBox(thiz,type){
        $(thiz).removeClass('active');
        $('.share_info').hide();
    }

                comments.getCommentList(0,3);

        function getCommentsNum(){

    function getNowDate () {
        var compareDate = new Date("2024-04-10 14:05:36");
        var currentDate = new Date();
        var timeDiff = currentDate.getTime() - compareDate.getTime();
        var secondsDiff = Math.floor(timeDiff / 1000);
        return secondsDiff;
    }

    function nowDateEnd(){
        var now = new Date("2024-04-10 14:05:36");
        var hours = now.getHours();
        var minutes = now.getMinutes();
        var seconds = now.getSeconds();
        var totalSeconds = (hours * 60 * 60) + (minutes * 60) + seconds;
        var secondDiff = (24 * 60 * 60) - totalSeconds;
        return secondDiff;
    }
    let nowdate = getNowDate();
    let $timeDiff = nowdate; //发布时间距离当前时间的差值(秒数)
    let nowDateEnds = nowDateEnd();
    let $secondDiff = nowDateEnds; //发布时间距离第二天的差值

    if($timeDiff < 60){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+'刚刚');
    }

    if($timeDiff < 3600){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+round($timeDiff / 60)+'分钟前');
    }

    if($timeDiff < 86400){
        if($timeDiff > $secondDiff){
            $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ '1天前');
        }
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ round($timeDiff / 3600)+'小时前');
    }
    if($timeDiff < $secondDiff + 86400*7){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ Math.ceil(($timeDiff - $secondDiff) / 86400)+'天前');
    }
</script>

            <p class="intro" style="white-space: pre-line">
                                                <br>
                    做起来很简单 夏天胃口不好，这样的海鲜粥再合适不过！食材可以根据自己的情况调整，山药要戴着手套操作不然手会很痒
给孩子吃不用加白胡椒，大人吃加一点会更好吃哦

                <!-- 步骤 -->
                <div class="step">
            <h2 class="mini-title">干贝虾仁粥的做法</h2>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement2" data-snum="2" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/yuan_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/yuan_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/4/3/f/200_43e9bc2f81eaf2c6fb1972f8d4ebd8ff.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解1" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤1</p>
                    干贝提前三小时冷藏泡发备用，山药要戴手套处理切成丁，胡萝卜切丁。其他材料洗净备用，青菜叶切碎
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement3" data-snum="3" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/yuan_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/yuan_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/5/e/f/200_5ee09c7811cfa29cacc023a2c39e719f.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解2" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤2</p>
                    锅里加水800克，煮开加入80克大米中火边搅拌边煮，煮到粘稠状。加生抽跟糖调味
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement4" data-snum="4" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/yuan_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/yuan_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/e/c/0/200_ec89499670f0d6c3b6b8c264359d39b0.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解3" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤3</p>
                    加入干贝，虾仁，山药，姜丝，青豆，胡萝卜，蟹腿菇，全部倒入锅里。中火煮三分钟。要一直搅拌。
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement5" data-snum="5" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/yuan_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/yuan_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/d/c/b/200_dc7f2d5e07c9466422033169e750149b.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解4" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤4</p>
                    最后放入青菜叶，搅拌均匀，加松鲜鲜香油。大人可以加白胡椒主要是去腥増鲜，小孩可以选择不加。
                </div>
            </div>
                        <div class="stepcont clearfix">
                <a class="cboxElement cboxElement6" data-snum="6" rel="recipe_img" href="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/yuan_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg" data-origin="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/yuan_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg">
                                            <img class="br8" src="https://cp1.douguo.com/upload/caiku/1/8/1/200_18932a7d2926578148ac661b63ab8211.jpg" alt="海鲜干贝粥的做法图解5" width="200" height="200" />
                                    </a>
                <div class="stepinfo">
                    <p>步骤5</p>
                    完成
                </div>
            </div>
                    </div>
                        <!-- 小贴士 -->

            <h2 class="mini-title">干贝虾仁粥的烹饪技巧</h2>
            <p><br>做菜好吃都有技巧，我的每道菜都有小妙招，大家搜索“豆果”可以直接查看我的菜谱！</p>

<script>
    function showShareBox(thiz,type){
        $(thiz).addClass('active');
        $('.share_info').removeClass('wechat weibo qq');
        if(type == 1){
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至微信');
            $('.share_info').addClass('wechat');
        } else if(type == 2){
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至微博');
            $('.share_info').addClass('weibo');
        }else{
            $('.share_info p').text('分享至QQ');
            $('.share_info').addClass('qq');
        }
        $('.share_info').show();
    }
    function hideShareBox(thiz,type){
        $(thiz).removeClass('active');
        $('.share_info').hide();
    }
    var comments = '';
    $(function(){
        $.ajax({
            url: "/login/user",
            data:"",
            success:function(res) {
                var user=res.data.user;
                comments = new Comments("3300888",'cook',user,'wHsgB8jFmv7U8mQkkpyE4Zxi6yKHNNoeHcByDQnw',3,$('.readMore'));
                comments.getCommentList(0,3);
                // getCommentsNum();
            }
        })
        // $.ajax({
        //     url: "/cookformat/"+"3300888",
        //     data:"",
        //     success:function(res) {
        //         $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+res.data);
        //     }
        // })
        function getCommentsNum(){
            var data = { type: 'cook', 'id': 3300888, sort: "desc" };
            $.ajax({
                url: '/comment/list/0/3',
                type: 'get',
                data: data,
                success: function success(res) {
                    var total = res.data.total;
                    if(total > 1){
                        $('.readMore').show();
                    }
                }
            });
        }
        $('.readMore').click(function(){
            $('.toast').show();
        })
    })
    function getNowDate () {
        var compareDate = new Date("2024-04-10 14:05:36");
        var currentDate = new Date();
        var timeDiff = currentDate.getTime() - compareDate.getTime();
        var secondsDiff = Math.floor(timeDiff / 1000);
        return secondsDiff;
    }

    function nowDateEnd(){
        var now = new Date("2024-04-10 14:05:36");
        var hours = now.getHours();
        var minutes = now.getMinutes();
        var seconds = now.getSeconds();
        var totalSeconds = (hours * 60 * 60) + (minutes * 60) + seconds;
        var secondDiff = (24 * 60 * 60) - totalSeconds;
        return secondDiff;
    }
    let nowdate = getNowDate();
    let $timeDiff = nowdate; //发布时间距离当前时间的差值(秒数)
    let nowDateEnds = nowDateEnd();
    let $secondDiff = nowDateEnds; //发布时间距离第二天的差值

    if($timeDiff < 60){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+'刚刚');
    }

    if($timeDiff < 3600){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+round($timeDiff / 60)+'分钟前');
    }

    if($timeDiff < 86400){
        if($timeDiff > $secondDiff){
            $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ '1天前');
        }
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ round($timeDiff / 3600)+'小时前');
    }
    if($timeDiff < $secondDiff + 86400*7){
        $('#creattime').html('创建时间 : '+ Math.ceil(($timeDiff - $secondDiff) / 86400)+'天前');
    }
</script>
